    <section data-content-field="main-content" id="page" role="main">
     <!-- CATEGORY NAV -->
     <div data-collection-id="" id="projectPages">
      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/gold-leaf-on-glass/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Gold Leaf on Glass
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          We design and execute a wide variety of gold leaf lettering and graphics on glass ranging from 23k gold leaf to silver, copper and Dutch leaf.
         </p>
         <p>
          Traditional gold leafing is typically done on the interior side of the glass, in reverse. Because of this, consideration needs to be given to wether the glass is tinted or double paned, which will affect the final look of the art work.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/hand-painted-wood-signs/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Hand Painted Wood Signs
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          From large scale vintage billboard signage to small interior decor pieces, we produce a wide range of hand painted wooden signs.
         </p>
        </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/the-cranberries-ghost-sign-limerick-ireland/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         The Cranberries Ghost Sign: Limerick, Ireland
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <h1>
          A Renowned American sign painter is to come to Limerick in September to work on a public artwork that draws on the music of The Cranberries. Limerick Leader
         </h1>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          In September 2015, Sean and Kayleigh Starr were invited by the City of Limerick, Ireland to participate in the Elemental Arts Festival and to design and execute a large scale, original "ghost sign" project in association with the band The Cranberries which is on display in Limerick's City Center. Starr also had work on display in Elemental Art's &amp; Culture Exhibition tiled Love Letters from Limerick curated by Tom Collins, which opened on September 18, 2015 at the Limerick School for Arts &amp; Design's FabLab Gallery.
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          The "ghost sign" project was a collaboration that was arranged and organized by Irish sign artist Tom Collins, who also assisted in the execution of the piece with artists Sean Starr, Kayleigh Starr and Simon Robinson. The piece is now on permanent display at the Limerick Institute of Technology in Limerick, Ireland
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Photo courtesy of Fusion Shooters. Sean Starr with Noel Hogan and Fergal Lawler of The Cranberries in Limerick, Ireland.
          </em>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/toadies-heretics-album-cover-art/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Toadies: Heretics Album Cover Art
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          Starr Studios' work graces the cover of the band The Toadies album Heretics which was released on September 18, 2015. The design was also incorporated into several pieces of apparel including t-shirts and belt buckles. The piece was commissioned by the band for the front cover art and executed on glass and features verre eglomise reverse glass gilding.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/gap-pico-de-gap-national-ad-campaign/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Gap: Pico de Gap National Ad Campaign
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          In 2011 Starr Studios was commissioned by GAP Jeans to hand paint 3 taco trucks that were launched in Los Angeles, San Francisco and Chicago. The trucks were teamed with celebrity chefs to celebrate the 1969 collection. In addition, the studio was commissioned to execute multiple in store graphics at several Gap store locations in the Los Angeles area as well as signage for the Gap booth at Bonnaroo Music Festival.
         </p>
         <p>
          "Gap clothing brand, the purveyors of classic blue jeans and knitwear, launched the Pico de Gap taco truck to celebrate the launch of creative director Rosella Giuliani's new 1969 collection." Los Angeles Times
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/gordy-sons-houston/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Gordy &amp; Sons Outfitters
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          In 2017 Starr Studios was commissioned to create classic styled 23k gilded glass throughout the Gordy &amp; Sons Outfitters showroom in Houston, Texas. The project included hand drawn acanthus leaf border details, custom designed monograms and a large scale, genuine silver leaf and 23k antiqued verre eglomise mirror installed in the showroom elevator and exterior signage.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/paul-chris-andrews-car-collection/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Paul &amp; Chris Andrews Car Collection
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          In 2014 Starr Studios was commissioned by the Andrews Family of Fort Worth to create dozens of large scale art installations at the Paul &amp; Chris Andrews Car Museum in Fort Worth.
         </p>
         <p>
          "Paul Andrews knows what its like when the rubber hits the road. He also knows what its like to overcome a setbackand how to build something to show for it. Andrews founded the Fort Worth specialty electronics broker TTI (formerly Tex-tronics) in 1971 after General Dynamics laid him off, making him collateral damage from the grounding of an F-111 fighter jet project. Shortly after TTI launchedand well before he sold the company to Warren Buffetts Berkshire Hathaway in 2007Andrews began building an exotic car collection, acquiring four-wheeled beauties from far-flung corners of the world. He has spent 41 years growing that collection and has put the vehicles on display in a Fort Worth museum with his son, Chris." D Magazine
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/j-hall-tattoo-dallas/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         J. Hall &amp; Co. Tattoo
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          n 2012 tattoo artist Josh Hall commissioned Starr Studios for branding, sign painting and gilded glass for J. Hall &amp; Co. Gentleman Tattooers located on South Lamar in Dallas. The project has evolved over the years with new artwork being added each year to the exterior and interior.
          <em>
           Photos by Daniel Driensky and Sarah Reyes for the Dallas Observer.
          </em>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/indian-motorcycles-black-hills-beast/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Indian Motorcycle's Black Hills Beast
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          In July of 2015 Starr Studios was commissioned by Indian Motorcycles to design and execute the paintwork on a 2015 Indian Scout motorcycle to pay tribute to Indian's history in hillclimb motorcycle racing. The bike was built by Indianmotorcycles.net and made its debut at the 75th Anniversary Sturgis Motorcycle Rally in Sturgis, South Dakota on August 3, 2015 with an attendance that exceeded 1,000,000.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Photos courtesy of Indian Motorcycle and Indianmotorcycles.net
          </em>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/car-collection-painted-signs/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Flying A Garage
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          In 2014 Starr Studios was commissioned by the Andrews Family of Fort Worth to create dozens of large scale art installations at the Paul &amp; Chris Andrews Car Museum in Fort Worth.
         </p>
         <p>
          "Paul Andrews knows what its like when the rubber hits the road. He also knows what its like to overcome a setbackand how to build something to show for it. Andrews founded the Fort Worth specialty electronics broker TTI (formerly Tex-tronics) in 1971 after General Dynamics laid him off, making him collateral damage from the grounding of an F-111 fighter jet project. Shortly after TTI launchedand well before he sold the company to Warren Buffetts Berkshire Hathaway in 2007Andrews began building an exotic car collection, acquiring four-wheeled beauties from far-flung corners of the world. He has spent 41 years growing that collection and has put the vehicles on display in a Fort Worth museum with his son, Chris." D Magazine
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

      <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/jesse-james-chopper/">
       <div class="project-meta">
        <h2 class="project-title">
         Jesse James Chopper
        </h2>
        <div class="project-description">
         <p>
          In 2014 Starr was commissioned by the Andrews Family of Fort Worth to customize a one of a kind Jesse James Chopper at the Paul &amp; Chris Andrews Car Museum in Fort Worth. The design was executed using 23k gold leaf and lettering enamels.
         </p>
         <p>
          "Paul Andrews knows what its like when the rubber hits the road. He also knows what its like to overcome a setbackand how to build something to show for it. Andrews founded the Fort Worth specialty electronics broker TTI (formerly Tex-tronics) in 1971 after General Dynamics laid him off, making him collateral damage from the grounding of an F-111 fighter jet project. Shortly after TTI launchedand well before he sold the company to Warren Buffetts Berkshire Hathaway in 2007Andrews began building an exotic car collection, acquiring four-wheeled beauties from far-flung corners of the world. He has spent 41 years growing that collection and has put the vehicles on display in a Fort Worth museum with his son, Chris." D Magazine
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

            <div class="image-card sqs-dynamic-text-container">
             <div class="image-title-wrapper">
              <div class="image-title sqs-dynamic-text">
               <p>
                About Us
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="image-subtitle-wrapper">
              <div class="image-subtitle sqs-dynamic-text">
               <p>
                We have been designing and making hand painted signs for over 30 years and our studio was featured in the documentary film and book "Sign Painters" as well as on the Discovery Channel, NBC Television, Food Network, Juxtapoz Magazine, Art Forum, Los Angeles Times, Dallas Observer, Houston Press, Fort Worth Magazine, Limerick Post and This Old House. Select clients include Sony Music, NBC Television, The GAP, Starbucks, Indian Motorcycle as well as Reese Witherspoon, Fleetwood Mac's Lindsay Buckingham, and the bands The Cranberries and The Toadies.
               </p>
